 Ekadashi fast is very important in Hinduism
 caitra maas kii shukla ekadshi ko kaamada ekadshi kaha jaataa he
 According to Padma Purana, Lord Vishnu is worshiped on the day of Kamada Ekadashi
 kaamada ekadshi vrath ke prabhaav se manushya pret yoni se mukti paata he
 On the day of Kamada Ekadashi fasting, according to the Hindu scriptures, on the day of Kamada Ekadashi, fasting should be purified with bathing
 iske pashchaat bhagwaan vishnu kaa fal, phool, doodh, panchamrita, til aadi se pujan karne kii salaah di gai he
 One should not sleep at night, but should spend the night doing bhajan-kirtan
 agle din yani paaran ke din punah pujan kar brahman ko bhojan karana chahie
 After taking Dakshina, after leaving the Brahmin, he should take food and open a fast
 kaamada ekadshi vrath kaa mahatvakaamada ekadshi vrath kaa vidhi- vidhaan dwaara paalan karne se manushya ke sabhi paap dur ho jate hai
 The same virtue is also achieved by listening to or narrating the story of Kamada Ekadashi fast

 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he) There is a wave of happiness in India with the news of the death of Maulana Masood Azhar, the most wanted terrorist of India and the leader of jaish-e-mohammed
 lekin maut ke saudagar masood ajahar kii maut kii khabar ek chhalaava bhi ho sakati he
 Because the Pakistan government and the ISI were under constant attack since the Pulwama attack
 antarrashtriya dabaav or bharat ke pukhta saboot uske liye pareshaani kaa sabab ban gaye the
 There can be four things behind this move of Pakistan
 1
 PAK made Masood the underground! The news of the death of Masood Azhar, the boss of terror, spread rapidly throughout the world
 dekhte hi dekhte yah khabar soshal media par chaa gai
 In India, she started trending in the top on Twitter
 lekin aatanki masood ajahar ke achaanak marane kii khabar par yakeen kar paanaa mushkil he
 After the Pulwama attack and the air strike, there is a lot of apprehension that the Pakistani government and ISI may have underground the terrorist Masood Azhar himself due to the increasing pressure
 2
 The drama of the death of Masuz Azhar! There were attacks on Pakistan from all sides regarding terrorist Masood Azhar
 us par masood ke khilaaf karrwai karne kaa dabaav bhi badhata ja rahaa tha
 At the same time, India also handed over the dossier to Pakistan, which had strong evidence of Jaish being involved in the Pulwama attack
 lihaaja paak kii bebas or laachaar sarkaar ne duniya main bhram failaane ke liye moulana masood ajahar kii maut kaa drama rach diya
 Under a conspiracy, the news of his hospitalization first came and then suddenly his death was made viral
 3
 Pak itself imposed Masood! India exposes jaish-e-mohammed by handing the dossier to Pakistan
 pulavama hamale ke saare saboot pakistan ke saamne rakh die
 Earlier, Masood's terrorist organization has carried out several major attacks in India
 jisase pakistan kaa doharaa charitra ujagar ho chukaa he
 India put all the evidence of those attacks and conspiracies in front of the world and showed the real face of the terrorist country to the world
 mana ja rahaa he ki paak or iesai pehle to aatank ke aakaa masood ko khud aatank failaane ke liye istemaal karte rahe lekin uski karatootein ujagar ho jane ke baad usase pallaa jhaad liya
 There are apprehensions that Pakistan itself has killed Masood Azhar
 4
 Masood killed in Balakot Air Strike! Pakistan's government army and ISI seem helpless and helpless
 sarkaar imran khan nahin balki fouj or ISI hi chalaate hai
 In such a situation, there is a possibility that terrorist leader Masood Azhar may have been killed in an air strike of the Indian Air Force in Balakot
 lekin pakistan khabar ko chupaane kii koshish kar rahaa ho
 Because till now Pakistan is denying that there were terrorist hideouts in Balakot
 yaa unhen indian air force ne tabah kar diya he
 It is feared that only after Masood was killed, the Pak government spread false news of his illness
 or phir achaanak elaan kar diya ki wo beemaari ke chalate maaraa gaya
 Confirming that he was killed in an air strike can be a big problem for Pakistan

 tippaniyan There are currently 24 categories in this list
 inamen ucch nyaayalayon ke nyaayadhish, saansad, varisht adhikari, vyapaaree, patrkaar or khilaadi shaamil hai
 In the past, India and Pakistan have expressed concern over the elimination of visa requirements for security reasons

 18-varshiya rubi ko somvaar ko jamaanat mil gai
 He was arrested by the Bihar Police, which was heavily disputed
 baad main use juvenil home main bhej diya gaya or uski jamaanat yachika do baar naamanzoor kar di gai thi
 The Juvenile Justice Board had said that Ruby Rai had committed a serious crime in association with others to become the 12th Arts Topper
 rubi raay kii pole us vakt khuli jab tivi intervyuu main usne kaha ki raajnneeti vigyaan (polytical science) main khaanaa pakaane ke bare main padhaayaa jaataa he
 The comments is maamle ne khub tool pakadaa
 Later about 30 people including several senior education officers and the principal of that college were arrested
 ri-test or intervyuu main rubi ek bhi sawaal kaa jawaab nahin de pai thi

 rashtriya suraksha salaahkaar ajit dobhaal ne seemaa vivaad hal karne ke tareekon par charchaa karne ke liye china ke unke samakaksh yang jichi se yahaan 19wein daur kii salanaa vaarta kii, jisamen yah faisla hua
 The two held detailed, thorough and candid discussions on the 3,488-km-long Line of Actual Control (LAC), which is strained between the two sides due to non-delimitation
 china ke videsh mantralay ke ek bayaan ke anusaar, donon pakshon ne seemaa ke sawaal kaa hal nikaalane ke liye shantipurna vaarta karne par kaayam rahane kii sahmati jataai
 They will try to arrive at a fair, rational and mutually acceptable solution
 dobhaal or jichi seemaa vivaad par vaarta karne ke liye apane-apane deshon ke vishesh pratinidhi hai
 They additionally have the right to discuss all complex bilateral, regional and international issues
 yang ne baithak main apane udghaatan bhaashan main dobhaal kaa swaagat karte hue kaha, 'aapaki yatra bhartiya paksh dwaara is baithak ko die jane vaale mahatv ko or china tathaa bharat ke bich ranneetik saajhedaari ko or protsaahit karne ke prayaason ko puri tarah rekhaankit karti he
 'he said,' china-india relations are of special importance
 china is mahatvapurn avasar kaa istemaal dwipaksheeya sambandhon, seemaa ke prashn, kshetreey or antarrashtriya muddon tathaa anya saajha hiton ke muddon par bhartiya paksh ke saath vyapak, gahan vichaar-vimarsh ke liye karne ke lihaaj se taiyaar he
 ' dobhaal ne apni tippanee main unke or yang ke bich hui anaupchaarik vaarta ke mahatv ko bataaya or kaha ki baatcheet dimag se nahin balki dil se ho rahi he
 The statement issued by the official Xinhua news agency said that the two sides will deal with the differences appropriately
 donon pakshon ne yah raay saajha kii ki china-bharat ke sambandhon kii vyapak sambhaavnaaen hai
 It said that bilateral relations have entered a new period of extensive and rapid development since the successful visit of Chinese President Xi Chinping to India in 2014 and Prime Minister Narendra Modi's visit to China in 2015
 bayaan ke anusaar, donon pakshon ke bich bani aam-sahmati ko lagu karnaa chahie, ucchstareey samvaad badhanaa chahie, sahyog kii kshamta badhaani chahie or china-bharat sambandhon ko ucch str tak pahunchaana chahie

 ab party nirnay legi
